  P2-P3: 长时间实验指导

以下实验需重训练（数小时），请参考以下命令手动执行：

  [P2] SPN σ 消融:
    # σ=0.001
    sed -i 's/NOISE_STD = 0.01/NOISE_STD = 0.001/' apjf_src/spn_config.py
    /home/oyp/miniconda3/envs/apjf/bin/python apjf_src/train_spn.py
    cp weights/spn_extractor_best.pth weights/spn_extractor_sigma_0.001.pth
    # σ=0.05
    sed -i 's/NOISE_STD = 0.001/NOISE_STD = 0.05/' apjf_src/spn_config.py
    /home/oyp/miniconda3/envs/apjf/bin/python apjf_src/train_spn.py
    cp weights/spn_extractor_best.pth weights/spn_extractor_sigma_0.05.pth

  [P3] Oracle baseline:
    见 run_supplement_experiments.sh 末尾注释
